Arab Spring.  A man self-immolates in front of the Egyptian parliament.  Another self-immolates in Alexandria.  This is the first such event in Egypt following the revolution in Tunisia.
Arab Spring.  A man self-immolates in front of the Egyptian parliament.  Another self-immolates in Alexandria.  This is the first such event in Egypt following the revolution in Tunisia.
Arab Spring.  The 2011 Egyptian Revolution.  An uprising triggered by lack of jobs, food prices, and authoritarianism.  The uprising features marches, riots, sit-ins, and strikes.  Police and military forces respond with deadly force.
Arab Spring.  Mass prison escapes occur during the revolution.  Soldiers arrest or kill a large number of the escapees.
